		<div class="g_bubble desc">
<b>Hanazawa Kana</b>, born 25.02.1989, in Tokyo, Japan, is a voice 
actress (seiyuu), actress, singer, former child actress and talent 
represented by <a href="http://anidb.net/cr1451">Office Osawa</a>. She is notable for voice acting leading roles for several anime television shows and other anime-related media in Japan.<br>
<br>
Hanazawa originally became a child actress at the age of 8. Amongst 
other roles she stared in the well-known TV school show Appare Sanma 
Daisensei (やっぱりさんま大先生) and the TV series Gakko no Sensei (ガッコの先生). At 
that time she was contracted to <a href="http://anidb.net/cr1485">Big Apple</a> and later to Five Eight (ファイブ☆エイト) and Smile Monkey (スマイルモンキー).<br>
<br>
In 2006 she was selected for a major role in <a href="http://anidb.net/cr804">TV Tokyo</a>'s anime mecha series <a href="http://anidb.net/a4178">Zegapain</a>. She was playing the main character's childhood friend, <a href="http://anidb.net/ch2814">Kaminagi Ryouko</a>,
 and her performance was one of the main reasons for the character's 
popularity amongst fans. It was afterwards that she came under contract 
at prestigious voice acting talent agency <a href="http://anidb.net/cr1451">Office Osawa</a> in 2007.<br>
<br>
Most of her roles are that of young girls. Though in <a href="http://anidb.net/a4919">Potemayo</a>, she played the <a href="http://anidb.net/ch7609">main character</a>, a small, cute creature. She received the role mainly because <a href="http://anidb.net/cr16776">Ogataya Haruka</a>,
 the creator of the original manga, was a big supporter of hers at 
auditions for the anime's cast, saying her version of Potemayo's sounds 
was just right for the character. Following Potemayo, she had twice a 
leading role in <a href="http://anidb.net/cr754">Hal Film Maker</a> productions.<br>
<br>
Hanazawa shares a trait with many of the characters she voices, as she 
is usually shy of strangers and has problems in the beginning of 
interviews and radio shows. She likes taking baths and her special 
skills are mimicry, magic and storytelling.<br>
<br>
Hanazawa has a four years younger brother. In April, 2007 she started to
 attend university in addition to her usual work as voice actress.
		</div>
